<rating>1<//rating>< Text>
DO NOT rent a car from here. I seldom write reviews, but this place felt like a con job.

I'll admit, it started off nice enough, with a very helpful and kind representative helping me rent a car after some jerk ran a red light and totaled mine. She made it sound like a favor was being done by only charging a $300 deposit instead of a $500 one, given my situation.

Fast forward 2 weeks when I go to return the car and settle the bill, and a different person is at the desk. Despite SPECIFICALLY asking to NOT pay for extra insurance (because we all know that's a scam if you already have private car insurance), they charged $17 extra dollars per day (on top of the "$25/day" rate for the car). Never again will I give this place business.

It seemed like the guy at the desk knew it was a scam- I could tell from his reaction that he was used to people reacting as I did (with outrage at hidden fees that were about 2/3 the price of the original rental..ON TOP of base price).

If you see someone with a sign picketing in front of this shady business, it might be me! Know that there are MANY options/competitors in the area, and I can't imagine that any of them would be so disappointing.< /Text>

< text>
I decided to take a chance and rent from them to save a few bucks on a quick personal trip to San Diego. They were about $20 cheaper for a two day rental. The shuttle from the airport was a bit of an inconvenience, but the shuttle back to the airport wasn't that much out of the way at all as their office is on the way to the rental car center. The fees they quoted me on the reservation did not match my final bill. It was a difference of less than $2, so I did not fight it, but any professional establishment would not have this problem. I suspect they fudge the calculations on the reservation to hide their "internet fee". The office is far from impressive. Their was a swarm of fruit flies right in the middle of the room and the letting for the logo on the wall weren't even level. The pickup and drop off process went well, and the car I received was what you'd expect from any other rental company. The only complaint I have, is that they gave it to me without a full tank, which basically means I had to pay for the gas that the last guy didn't buy, and that guy was probably charged twice what it was worth.<//text>

<review>I feel obligated to write this review to warn you about consumer fraud by Pacific Rent a Car. The one star is for the excellent trap they designed. Bear with me and you will learn how they charged me $562 for missing $15 worth of toll.
As a visitor to California, I was not aware of the electronic toll roads which did not have any toll booth.  A few weeks later, $562 charge from Pacific mysteriously appeared on my credit card.  It turned out we missed three tolls for total about $15. In addition to the toll penalty of $172, Pacific charged me $375 processing fee for the ‚Äúcitations ‚Äú!!  Pacific made $375 out of this. Why is it a trap?
1)When I picked up the car, there was no mentioning of any toll arrangement by the agent or on the contract. They did NOT provide any device such as Fastrack on the car to pay toll.
The story does not end here.
2)I then called the state toll road agent, the person explained I DO NOT have to pay the penalty. If the customer could simply set up a Fastrack account retrospectively and pay for the tolls, penalty would be forgive. But Pacific has to first call the toll agent to reverse the payment of $172 penalty they already paid without my consent to get the money back. I called and also emailed Pacific. Pacific REFUSED to reverse the charge and get the money back!! They still want to make this into ‚Äúcitations‚Äù, so that they could charge me $375 processing fee!

I brought my dog here who had a cough and they were planning on doing xrays and blood tests... i asked for antibiotics if possible to start with, which they agreed to do. Initially they were going to charge 600 dollars.... for a cough.
Then I came to pick up the medication which was 92 dollars, only to find out that they charged twice for the antibiotics.... which they reversed, but this took 30 minutes to do. Very unprofessional and lengthy service for a simple issue.

They responded and were very kind by apologizing and calling and checking up on our dog. It was the initial experience which was unprofessional, but I am happy with how they have handled follow up and the kindness they have shown.</Review>

< Name>
Lindsay Gilliam<//Name>
< date>
1564684637682</date>
<rating>5< /rating>< Text>
My dog has unfortunately had a rough summer. It started with an embedded fox tail in his foot, then a couple weeks later a pretty serious abscess on his hip. When I called and told them what was going on, they said I could come right down. Not sure how this abscess formed, he hadn't suffered an injury, so thinking maybe another fox tail. Dr Murphy performed surgery but found no fox tail. She cleaned out the infection and gave him antibiotics. We went back yesterday to have the stitches removed, and my doggy ended up needing the surgery AGAIN, still no fox tail. It's hard, because there isn't really an answer at this point to why this abscess is there and why it's not healing correctly. It could be bacterial, they said, so my dog had a different type of antibiotic administered in a shot that lasts 2 weeks, which is nice. It's clear that they're doing everything they can with what seems to be a really explainable situation. Dr Murphy and the staff at Brighton Greens Vet have been really great. The Dr calls after every procedure and explains to me in detail how it went and what was done. She answers my questions. And while repeated veterinary visits/surgery is NOT cheap, the prices have been fair. Especially the last time, going in again since the wound didn't heal properly, they managed to stick to what was a very reasonable estimate. Anyhow, I really appreciate that even though the situation with my dog totally sucks, they've done their best to make it as bearable as possible. The staff is super compassionate, nice, friendly and accommodating. We will continue coming here, and definitely recommend Brighton Greens Veterinary Hospital!< /Text>

< text>
I would like to start out by saying that the food at Tapatios is delicious, and we have been going there for a while now. I love the siete mares soup!  I generally get the same lady and she knows my voice, what I like to order, is pleasant. However this last visit will unfortunately be our last. I understand tough days, and that people make mistakes , but what I cannot understand is poor customer service, and valuing a few dollars over keeping a customer. I called in our order, we picked it up after a long day.out. When we got home, I quickly realized that they had given me the wrong soup. I called in and spoke to a man that didn‚Äôt seem like he felt bad about this mixup, but said to bring the soup back to exchange it. I figured, he might just be busy, or frustrated that the lady in the front, whom I had never seen before, mixed it up. So, I was understanding, and even apologized to him and said I was sure it was a misunderstanding.  When we went back, there was no parking so we had to park down the street, and I had to walk to the restaurant. I get there and the lady barely apologized and told me that she needed to charge me $4 more dollars. I know they are a small mom and pop, but I have never heard of an establishment making a mistake and then charging the customer for it. I explained that my purse was in the car down the road, and asked her politely if she was serious about charging me for their mistake. She barely spoke to me, and I was getting very frustrated.  She was going over the prices and said that the soup I wanted was $12.95. I asked her, "wasn‚Äôt the soup $9.95", because that is what I remember it always being.  She said she didn‚Äôt know, and one of the men in the back said yeah, like 2 years ago, which I found to be quite rude. So I walked back to my car, got the card went back, expressed how I was unhappy that they would charge me after I had wasted my time going home, having to go back out and find a spot etc, and it wasn‚Äôt even my mistake. I know what I said, it‚Äôs the thing I order most from them. They gave me beef soup, I have never even heard of beef soup, and it doesn‚Äôt sound that appetizing, so I know I would have never said that. She barely paid attention to me, just scanned my card and handed me my food. I asked if the owner was around and she pointed at a person behind the wall that I couldn‚Äôt see, I asked if I could talk to them, but she just said he was busy talking to someone.  Someone else behind there must have heard me because a man came over and just looked at me.  I asked him if he was the manager, and he nodded. No name, no handshake, he just looked at me. I explained why I was upset, he said the lady heard beef soup. I explained that I didn‚Äôt say beef soup, that I go there all of the time, and that it was very upsetting that they would charge me extra for their mistake. He just said that that was their policy. The lack of empathy and customer service was quite shocking, especially from a man that said he was the owner. I told him "I guess I was going to have to find another taco shop to go to then", and walked away, to which I could hear him say that he was sorry. Which was the first time he had said it. I was pretty upset by this, I know it seems quite trivial given all the things that life can throw at you, but I honestly expected more from them.  I thought I was a good valued customer, but apparently not so much. I guess $4 bucks was worth losing a good loyal customer. It stinks too because they really do make the best siete mares I have ever had, but there is no way I would go back after the way I feel I was treated.  So to sum things up, the food is great, and I have had generally good experiences there, but just hope there is not a problem with your order because you might wind up having a similar experience than I‚Äôve had.  Then again, maybe not. I wish them and you the best of luck!< /text>
